NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, S. Deepak Kumar, Biological son of Thiru B. Sukumar, residing at Old No. 12A,
New No. 21A, Kalingarayan 1st Street, Cemetery Road, Old Washermenpet, Chennai-600 021,
by way of this public notice. I, inform that (late) Thiru P. Shanmugam, has legally adopted me
as his son on 29th day of March 1996 by way of registered deed bearing No. 116/1996 on the
Sub-Registrar Office, Royapuram, Chennai-13 my adopted father Thiru P. Shanmugam (late)
passed way on 11th September 2008. Here after I shall be known as S. DEEPAK KUMAR.

Chennai,
16th April 2012.

S. DEEPAK KUMAR.
